  ~new_tempo00 := real(ms_to_ticks(60000000)) / 960.

            %_repetition_interval_time[($i00 * 4096) + (($ii00 * 512) + $iii00)] := int((60000. / ~tempo) * (4. / real(%_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($i00 * 32) + (($ii00 * 4) + $iii00)])))
          end if
          inc($iii00)
        end while
        inc($ii00)
      end while
      inc($i00)
    end while
  end if

function c_set_background_animation0
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_bg), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "bg_ani_" & (($frame00 / 32) + 1))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_bg), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ($frame00 mod 32) - ((($frame00 mod 32) - (30 + abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(($frame00 / 32) - 3) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)))) .and. sh_right((30 + abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(($frame00 / 32) - 3) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))) - ($frame00 mod 32), 31)))
end function
function keyswitches_color_keys
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_RED)
    if(%_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] = 1)
      set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_ORANGE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function c_subarticulation_group_count0
  $group_count01 := 0
  if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id00]] = 2)
    $group_count01 := 6 * ((%subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id00]] * 3) + %subarticulations_trans_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id00]])
  else
    $group_count01 := (6 * %subarticulations_interval_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id00]]) * ((%subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id00]] * %subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id00]]) * (1 + %subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id00]]))
  end if
  $ret00 := $group_count01
end function
function c_update_keyswitch_selection0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_control_par(%swi_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    set_control_par_str(%swi_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !_articulation_names[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    set_key_pressed(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_RED)
    if(%_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] = 1)
      set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_ORANGE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE) = $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_articulation_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_humanization[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_articulation_humanize & " ms")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_release[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_articulation_release & " ms")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
      inc($i)
    end while
    $idx170002 := 0
    while($idx170002 <= (num_elements(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection) - 1)) 
      if($idx170002 # $selected_subarticulation)
        set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx170002], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
      else
        set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx170002], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
      end if
      inc($idx170002)
    end while
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    " & !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]])
    else
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    Empty")
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_solo_subarticulation), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_subarticulations_solo_states[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_volume & " dB")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_repetition_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 0) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 5)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 6))
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_tightness[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_tightness & " %")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
    if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 6)
      $mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed := %_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_repetition_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
    if(((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 1) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 2)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 4))
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_vibrato[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_vibrato & " %")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
    if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 2)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_trans_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_trans_volume & " dB")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_trans_speed & " %")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      $btn_subarticulation_trans_speed := %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed_auto[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed = 1)
        set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      end if
    end if
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 3) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
        else
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
        end if
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real(((%modulation_positions[0] * (1 + (sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31) .or. sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)))) - sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
    @txt_keyswitch_name := !_articulation_names[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
      inc($i)
    end while
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 3) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
        else
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
        end if
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real(((%modulation_positions[0] * (1 + (sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31) .or. sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)))) - sh_right(%modulation_positions[0] - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - %modulation_positions[0], 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
  end if
end function
function c_wait_or_zero0
  if($wait_time00 > 0)
    wait($wait_time00)
  end if
end function
function c_is_in_note_selection0
  $result01 := 0
  select($note_selection00)
    case 0
      $result01 := 1
    case 1
      $result01 := - sh_right(abs($idx160) - 1, 31)
    case 2
      $result01 := - sh_right(abs($idx160) - 1, 31) + - sh_right(abs($idx160 - 1) - 1, 31)
    case 3
      $result01 := (- sh_right(abs($idx160) - 1, 31) + (- sh_right(abs($idx160 - ($num_pressed_notes00 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes00, 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx160 - (($num_pressed_notes00 / 2) - 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes00, 31))
    case 4
      $result01 := (- sh_right(abs($idx160) - 1, 31) + (- sh_right(abs($idx160 - ($num_pressed_notes00 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes00, 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx160 - ((($num_pressed_notes00 - 2) / 2) + 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes00, 31))
    case 5
      $result01 := - sh_right(abs($idx160 - ($num_pressed_notes00 / 2)) - 1, 31)
    case 6
      $result01 := (((- sh_right(abs($idx160 - ($num_pressed_notes00 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes00, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx160 - (($num_pressed_notes00 / 2) - 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes00, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx160 - $num_pressed_notes00) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - ($num_pressed_notes00 + 1), 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx160 - (((($num_pressed_notes00 + 1) - 2) / 2) + 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - ($num_pressed_notes00 + 1), 31))
    case 7
      $result01 := (- sh_right(abs($idx160 - ($num_pressed_notes00 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes00, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($idx160 - (($num_pressed_notes00 / 2) - 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $num_pressed_notes00, 31))
    case 8

    case 10
      $result01 := - sh_right(abs($idx160 - ($num_pressed_notes00 - 1)) - 1, 31) + - sh_right(abs($idx160 - ($num_pressed_notes00 - 2)) - 1, 31)
    case 11

    case -2147483648 to 134217727
      $result01 := 0
  end select
  $is_in_note_selection_boolean := 1 + sh_right(abs($result01) - 1, 31)
end function
function c_event_list_get_articulation_event0
  $result22 := -1
  if(((((($instrument_slot40 >= 0) and ($instrument_slot40 < 1)) and ($keyswitch50 >= 0)) and ($keyswitch50 < 8)) and ($note80 >= 0)) and ($note80 < 128))
    $result22 := %_event_list[($instrument_slot40 * 1024) + (($keyswitch50 * 128) + $note80)]
  end if
  $ret30 := $result22
end function
function c_delay_buffer_add0
  $idx190 := search(%delay_buffer, -1)
  if($idx190 # -1)
    %delay_buffer[$idx190] := $articulation_id10
    %delay_buffer_instrument[$idx190] := $instrument40
    %delay_buffer_keyswitch[$idx190] := $keyswitch80
    %delay_buffer_subarticulation[$idx190] := $subarticulation40
    %delay_buffer_note[$idx190] := $note110
    %delay_buffer_velo[$idx190] := $velo00
    %delay_buffer_interval[$idx190] := $interval10
    %delay_buffer_countdown[$idx190] := $countdown00
    %delay_buffer_prev_note[$idx190] := $previous_note10
    $any_delay_event_queued := 1
  else
    message("WARNING: Delay Buffer Full")
  end if
end function
function c_articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id0
  $result34 := -1
  if($articulation_event_id00 >= 0)
    $result34 := %_articulation_event_list[($articulation_event_id00 * 4) + $subarticulation00]
  end if
  $ret40 := $result34
end function
function c_articulation_event_set_subarticulation_event_id0
  %_articulation_event_list[($articulation_event_id10 * 4) + $subarticulation10] := $subarticulation_event_id160
end function
function c_note_to_string0
  $reduced_note02 := 0
  $string03 := 0
  if(($instrument00 = 0) or ($instrument00 = 1))
    $reduced_note02 := ($note00 - 55) - $mnu_finger_position
    if($reduced_note02 >= 0)
      $string03 := $reduced_note02 / 7
    else
      $string03 := 0
    end if
  end if
  $string03 := $string03 - (($string03 - 3) .and. sh_right(3 - $string03, 31))
  $ret50 := $string03
end function
function c_articulations_note_off0
  $i60 := 0
  $release_offset00 := 0
  $ks10 := 0
  while($ks10 <= 7) 
    $ret30 := $_ret1600
    $instrument_slot40 := $instrument_slot10
    $keyswitch50 := $ks10
    $note80 := $note50
    $result22 := $result200
    call c_event_list_get_articulation_event0
    $_ret1600 := $ret30
    $instrument_slot10 := $instrument_slot40
    $ks10 := $keyswitch50
    $note50 := $note80
    if($_ret1600 # -1)
      $i60 := 0
      while($i60 <= 3) 
        if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument_slot10 * 32) + (($ks10 * 4) + $i60)] # -1)
          if((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument_slot10 * 32) + (($ks10 * 4) + $i60)]]] = 0) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument_slot10 * 32) + (($ks10 * 4) + $i60)]]] = 5))
            if(%subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument_slot10 * 32) + (($ks10 * 4) + $i60)]]] = 0)
              $release_offset00 := 500
            end if
          end if
          $ret30 := $result200
          $instrument_slot40 := $instrument_slot10
          $keyswitch50 := $ks10
          $note80 := $note50
          $result22 := $result210
          call c_event_list_get_articulation_event0
          $result200 := $ret30
          $instrument_slot10 := $instrument_slot40
          $ks10 := $keyswitch50
          $note50 := $note80
          $articulation_id10 := $result200
          $instrument40 := $instrument_slot10
          $keyswitch80 := $ks10
          $subarticulation40 := $i60
          $note110 := $note50
          $velo00 := -1
          $interval10 := 0
          $time10 := $ENGINE_UPTIME
          $countdown00 := $lookahead + $release_offset00
          $previous_note10 := -1
          $idx190 := $result210
          call c_delay_buffer_add0
          $result200 := $articulation_id10
          $instrument_slot10 := $instrument40
          $ks10 := $keyswitch80
          $i60 := $subarticulation40
          $note50 := $note110
        end if
        inc($i60)
      end while
      if((($instrument_slot10 # -1) and ($ks10 # -1)) and ($note50 # -1))
        if(%_event_list[($instrument_slot10 * 1024) + (($ks10 * 128) + $note50)] >= 0)
          %_event_list[($instrument_slot10 * 1024) + (($ks10 * 128) + $note50)] := -1
        end if
      end if
    end if
    inc($ks10)
  end while
end function

                            $previous_note10 := -1

                            call c_delay_buffer_add0
                          end if
                        end if
                      end if
                    end if
                  end if
                end if
                inc($i500)
              end while
              if($set_articulation_event_id001 = 1)
                %_event_list[($inst * 1024) + (($result000 * 128) + $i)] := $articulation_event_id401
                %articulation_event_instrument[$articulation_event_id401] := $inst
                %articulation_event_keyswitch[$articulation_event_id401] := $result000

                %_last_articulation_event[($inst * 1024) + (($result000 * 128) + $i)] := $articulation_event_id401
              end if
            end if

          end while
        else

          while($ks20 < 8) 
            $ret30 := $result000

              $i := $note50

            end if

          end while
        end if
        inc($inst)
      end while
    else
      if(%pressed_keys[$i] > 0)

        while($inst <= 0)

      end if

    end if

  end while
end function

function c_articulations_compute_level0
  ~subarticulation_modulation_strength02 := 0.
  $fade_in_start02 := %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($instrument_slot20 * 32) + (($keyswitch30 * 4) + $subarticulation20)]
  $fade_in_range02 := %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($instrument_slot20 * 32) + (($keyswitch30 * 4) + $subarticulation20)]
  $fade_out_end02 := %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($instrument_slot20 * 32) + (($keyswitch30 * 4) + $subarticulation20)]
  $fade_out_range02 := %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($instrument_slot20 * 32) + (($keyswitch30 * 4) + $subarticulation20)]
  if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$note60 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $fade_in_start02, $fade_out_end02))
    ~subarticulation_modulation_strength02 := 1.
    if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$note60 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $fade_in_start02, $fade_in_start02 + $fade_in_range02) and ($fade_in_range02 > 0))
      ~subarticulation_modulation_strength02 := real(%modulation_positions[$note60 * $use_polyphonic_modulation] - $fade_in_start02) / real($fade_in_range02)
    else
      if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$note60 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $fade_out_end02 - $fade_out_range02, $fade_out_end02) and ($fade_out_range02 > 0))
        ~subarticulation_modulation_strength02 := real($fade_out_end02 - %modulation_positions[$note60 * $use_polyphonic_modulation]) / real($fade_out_range02)
      end if
    end if
  end if
  $ret80 := int(1000000. * ((real(int(round(real(%_articulation_volume_min[($instrument_slot20 * 8) + $keyswitch30]) + (real(%_articulation_volume_max[($instrument_slot20 * 8) + $keyswitch30] - %_articulation_volume_min[($instrument_slot20 * 8) + $keyswitch30]) * pow(real(%modulation_positions[$note60 * $use_polyphonic_modulation]) / 127., (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($instrument_slot20 * 8) + $keyswitch30]) / 100.) + 1.))))) / 127.) * ~subarticulation_modulation_strength02))
end function

    set_event_par_arr(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id150], $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, $level10, 2)
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id150] # -1)
      set_event_par_arr(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id150], $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, $level10, 2)
    end if
  end if
  %subarticulation_event_level[$subarticulation_event_id150] := $level10
end function

function c_get_next_rr0
  $rr12 := 0
  if(%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument50 * 32) + (($keyswitch90 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx30)]]] = 0)
    $rr12 := (%_rr_data_idx[($instrument50 * 4096) + (($keyswitch90 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx30 * 128) + $note140))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument50 * 32) + (($keyswitch90 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx30)]]]
  else
    if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - %_rr_data_time[($instrument50 * 4096) + (($keyswitch90 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx30 * 128) + $note140))]) > %subarticulations_rrr_reset_time[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument50 * 32) + (($keyswitch90 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx30)]]])
      $rr12 := (%_rr_data_idx[($instrument50 * 4096) + (($keyswitch90 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx30 * 128) + $note140))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument50 * 32) + (($keyswitch90 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx30)]]]
    else
      $rr12 := %subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument50 * 32) + (($keyswitch90 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx30)]]] - ((%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument50 * 32) + (($keyswitch90 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx30)]]] - ((%_rr_data_idx[($instrument50 * 4096) + (($keyswitch90 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx30 * 128) + $note140))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument50 * 32) + (($keyswitch90 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx30)]]])) .and. sh_right(%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument50 * 32) + (($keyswitch90 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx30)]]] - ((%_rr_data_idx[($instrument50 * 4096) + (($keyswitch90 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx30 * 128) + $note140))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument50 * 32) + (($keyswitch90 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx30)]]]), 31))
    end if
    %_rr_data_time[($instrument50 * 4096) + (($keyswitch90 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx30 * 128) + $note140))] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  end if
  %_rr_data_idx[($instrument50 * 4096) + (($keyswitch90 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx30 * 128) + $note140))] := $rr12
  $ret90 := $rr12
end function

  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_sustain_release & " + " & $sli_sustain_release_offset & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_start), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_trans_start & " + " & $sli_trans_start_offset & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_trans_fadeIn) / 1000000.) * 750.) & " + " & int((real($sli_trans_fadeIn_offset) / 1000000.) * 750.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (round((real($sli_trans_volume) / 1000.) * pow(10., 2.)) / pow(10., 2.)) & " + " & (round((real($sli_trans_volume_offset) / 1000.) * pow(10., 2.)) / pow(10., 2.)) & " dB")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_fadeOut), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_trans_fadeOut) / 1000000.) * 1000.) & " + " & int((real($sli_trans_fadeOut_offset) / 1000000.) * 1000.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_wait), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_wait) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " + " & int((real($sli_sustain_wait_offset) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " + " & int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " ms")
end function

      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note00 * 25) + (abs($end_note00 - $start_note00) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note00 - $start_note00), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_fadeOut), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note00 * 25) + (abs($end_note00 - $start_note00) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note00 - $start_note00), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_wait), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_sus_wait_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note00 * 25) + (abs($end_note00 - $start_note00) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note00 - $start_note00), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note00 * 25) + (abs($end_note00 - $start_note00) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note00 - $start_note00), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_release_offset), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_sus_release_time_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note00 * 25) + (abs($end_note00 - $start_note00) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note00 - $start_note00), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_start_offset), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note00 * 25) + (abs($end_note00 - $start_note00) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note00 - $start_note00), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_fadeIn_offset), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note00 * 25) + (abs($end_note00 - $start_note00) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note00 - $start_note00), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_volume_offset), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note00 * 25) + (abs($end_note00 - $start_note00) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note00 - $start_note00), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_fadeOut_offset), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note00 * 25) + (abs($end_note00 - $start_note00) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note00 - $start_note00), 31) * 12)))])

      call update_authoring_labels
    else
      $authoring_interval_valid := 0
    end if
    if($authoring_interval_valid = 1)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    else
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
  end if
end function

  end if
end function

function c_subarticulation_play_note0
  $result601 := -1
  $idx2101 := 0
  while($idx2101 < 128) 
    if((%subarticulation_event_list[$idx2101] = -1) and (%subarticulation_event_last_used[$idx2101] < ($ENGINE_UPTIME - $lookahead)))
      $result601 := $idx2101
      $idx2101 := 128
    end if
    $idx2101 := $idx2101 + 1
  end while
  $subarticulation_event_id170 := $result601
  $idx2101 := 0
  $result601 := -1
  $transition_note_event02 := -1
  $transition_octave_event02 := -1
  $i122 := 0
  $ii22 := 0
  if(($subarticulation_event_id170 # -1) and ($subarticulation_idx00 # -1))
    if(($subarticulations_solo_states_any_active = 0) or (%_subarticulations_solo_states[($instrument10 * 32) + (($keyswitch00 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx00)] = 1))
      if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] # 2)
        $idx2101 := play_note($note17 + $transpose00, $velocity00, 0, 0)
        if($octave_layer00 # 0)
          $result601 := play_note(($note17 + $transpose00) + (12 * $octave_layer00), $velocity00, 0, 0)
        end if
        if((((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] = 0) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] = 3)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] = 5)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] = 6))
          if($previous_note00 >= 0)
            if((%articulation_event_instrument[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$previous_note00]] = $instrument10) and (%articulation_event_keyswitch[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$previous_note00]] = $keyswitch00))
              $subarticulation_event_id120 := $previous_note00
              $fade_time00 := 1000 - int((700. * real(%_loaded_subarticulations_tightness[($instrument10 * 32) + (($keyswitch00 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx00)])) / 100.)
              $stop_voice00 := 1
              call c_subarticulation_event_fade_out0
              $previous_note00 := $subarticulation_event_id120
            end if
          end if
        end if
        $subarticulation_event_id00 := $subarticulation_event_id170
        $event_id00 := $idx2101
        call c_subarticulation_event_set_event_id0
        $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id00
        $idx2101 := $event_id00
        $subarticulation_event_id18 := $subarticulation_event_id170
        $event_id10 := $result601
        call c_subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id0
        $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id18

        $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id90
        $subarticulation_event_id70 := $subarticulation_event_id170

        $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id70
        $i122 := 0
        while($i122 <= (%subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] - 1)) 
          $ii22 := 0
          while($ii22 <= 5) 
            $subarticulation_event_id80 := $subarticulation_event_id170
            $group00 := ((((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] + 1) + (((6 * %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]]) * %subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]]) * ($interval00 * (1 + %subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]])))) + ((($rr00 * %subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]]) * (%subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] + 1)) * 6)) + (($i122 * (%subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] + 1)) * 6)) + $ii22
            call c_subarticulation_event_allow_groups0
            $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id80

          end while
          inc($i122)
        end while
        $subarticulation_event_id110 := $subarticulation_event_id170

        $relative_bit00 := 1

            end if
          else
            message("REACHED MAX_SUBARTICULATIONS_IN_REPETITION_ENGINE")
          end if
          if((($ENGINE_UPTIME - $repetition_engine_start_time) mod %_repetition_interval_time[($instrument10 * 4096) + (($keyswitch00 * 512) + $subarticulation_idx00)]) > 5)

            $stop_voice00 := 0
            call c_subarticulation_event_fade_out0
            $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id120

          end if
        end if
      else
        $idx2202 := 0
        $end_note22 := 0
        $transition_note02 := -1
        $transition_type22 := -1
        $transition_dyn_layer02 := int((real($modulation00) / 1000000.) * 127.) / (128 / %subarticulations_trans_num[$subarticulation_id20])
        $offset12 := 0

            if(~transition_speed01 < 0.01)
              ~transition_speed01 := 0.
            end if
            ~transition_speed01 := 1. - ~transition_speed01

          end if

          else

          end if

                end if
              end if

            end while
            $i902 := 0
            while($i902 <= 7)

                %_last_transitions[($instrument10 * 256) + (($keyswitch00 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx00 * 8) + $i902))] := -1
              end if
              inc($i902)
            end while
            $_ret2802 := $result702
            if($_ret2802 = 1)
              $offset12 := 3
            else
              $result702 := -1
              $i902 := %_last_transitions_timecode[($instrument10 * 256) + (($keyswitch00 * 32) + ($subarticulation_idx00 * 8))]
              $i8002 := 0
              $i1002 := 0
              if($transition_type22 >= 0)
                $i1002 := 0
                while($i1002 <= 7) 
                  if(%_last_transitions[($instrument10 * 256) + (($keyswitch00 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx00 * 8) + $i1002))] = -1)
                    $result702 := $i1002
                    if($i902 > %_last_transitions_timecode[($instrument10 * 256) + (($keyswitch00 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx00 * 8) + $i1002))])

                else

                  %_last_transitions_timecode[($instrument10 * 256) + (($keyswitch00 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx00 * 8) + $i8002))] := $ENGINE_UPTIME

            end if
            $i902 := -1
            if(((((((($instrument10 >= 0) and ($instrument10 < 1)) and ($subarticulation_idx00 >= 0)) and ($subarticulation_idx00 < 4)) and ($transition_note02 >= 0)) and ($transition_note02 < 128)) and ($transition_dyn_layer02 >= 0)) and ($transition_dyn_layer02 < 2))

            change_vol($transition_note_event02, %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($instrument10 * 32) + (($keyswitch00 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx00)] * 1000, 1)
            if($transition_octave_event02 # -1)
              change_vol($transition_octave_event02, %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($instrument10 * 32) + (($keyswitch00 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx00)] * 1000, 1)
            end if
          end if
          $subarticulation_event_id70 := $subarticulation_event_id170
          call c_subarticulation_event_disallow_groups0
          $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id70
          $i122 := 0
          while($i122 <= (%subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] - 1)) 
            $ii22 := 0
            while($ii22 <= 5) 
              $subarticulation_event_id80 := $subarticulation_event_id170
              $group00 := (((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] + 1) + (6 * %subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]])) + ($i122 * 6)) + $ii22
              call c_subarticulation_event_allow_groups0
              $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id80
              inc($ii22)
            end while
            inc($i122)
          end while
          if(($authoring_page_active = 1) and ($btn_play_sustain = 0))
            fade_out($idx2101, 1000, 0)
            if($result601 # -1)
              fade_out($result601, 1000, 0)
            end if
          end if
        else
          $idx2101 := play_note($note17, $velocity00, 0, 0)
          if($octave_layer00 # 0)
            $result601 := play_note(($note17 + $transpose00) + (12 * $octave_layer00), $velocity00, 0, 0)
          end if
          $subarticulation_event_id00 := $subarticulation_event_id170
          $event_id00 := $idx2101
          call c_subarticulation_event_set_event_id0
          $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id00
          $idx2101 := $event_id00
          $subarticulation_event_id18 := $subarticulation_event_id170
          $event_id10 := $result601
          call c_subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id0
          $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id18
          $result601 := $event_id10
          $subarticulation_event_id90 := $subarticulation_event_id170
          call c_subarticulation_event_set_event_mark0
          $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id90
          $subarticulation_event_id70 := $subarticulation_event_id170
          call c_subarticulation_event_disallow_groups0
          $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id70
          $i122 := 0
          while($i122 <= (%subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] - 1)) 
            $ii22 := 0
            while($ii22 <= 5) 
              $subarticulation_event_id80 := $subarticulation_event_id170
              $group00 := ((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id20]] + 1) + ($i122 * 6)) + $ii22
              call c_subarticulation_event_allow_groups0
              $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id80
              inc($ii22)
            end while
            inc($i122)
          end while
          $subarticulation_event_id110 := $subarticulation_event_id170
          $volume00 := %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($instrument10 * 32) + (($keyswitch00 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx00)] * 1000
          $relative_bit00 := 1
          call c_subarticulation_event_change_vol0
          $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id110
          if(($authoring_page_active = 1) and ($btn_play_sustain = 0))
            fade_out($idx2101, 1000, 0)
            if($result601 # -1)
              fade_out($result601, 1000, 0)
            end if
          end if
        end if
      end if
    end if
    %subarticulation_event_note[$subarticulation_event_id170] := $note17
    %subarticulation_event_actual_note[$subarticulation_event_id170] := $note17 + $transpose00
    %subarticulation_event_subarticulation[$subarticulation_event_id170] := $subarticulation_id20
    %subarticulation_event_interval[$subarticulation_event_id170] := $interval00
    %subarticulation_event_octave_layer[$subarticulation_event_id170] := $octave_layer00
    $subarticulation_event_id140 := $subarticulation_event_id170
    $modulation10 := $modulation00
    call c_subarticulation_set_modulation0
    $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id140
    $modulation00 := $modulation10
    $subarticulation_event_id150 := $subarticulation_event_id170
    $level10 := $level00
    call c_subarticulation_set_level0
    $subarticulation_event_id170 := $subarticulation_event_id150
    $level00 := $level10
    %subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id170] := $transition_note_event02
    %subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id170] := $transition_octave_event02
    %subarticulation_event_last_used[$subarticulation_event_id170] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    %subarticulation_event_subarticulation_idx[$subarticulation_event_id170] := $subarticulation_idx00
  else
    message("WARNING: MAX_SUBARTICULATION_EVENTS reached")
  end if
  $ret100 := $subarticulation_event_id170
end function
function c_repetition_engine_update_tempo0
  ~new_tempo01 := real(ms_to_ticks(60000000)) / 960.
  if((~new_tempo01 # ~tempo) or ($NI_CALLBACK_TYPE # $NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER))
    ~tempo := ~new_tempo01
    $ii01 := 0
    $iii01 := 0
    $i01 := 0
    while($i01 <= 0) 
      $ii01 := 0
      while($ii01 <= 7) 
        $iii01 := 0
        while($iii01 <= 511) 
          if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($i01 * 32) + (($ii01 * 4) + $iii01)]]] = 6)
            %_repetition_interval_time[($i01 * 4096) + (($ii01 * 512) + $iii01)] := int((60000. / ~tempo) * (4. / real(%_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($i01 * 32) + (($ii01 * 4) + $iii01)])))
          end if
          inc($iii01)
        end while
        inc($ii01)
      end while
      inc($i01)
    end while
  end if
end function
function c_subarticulation_browser_load_category0
  $i22 := 0
  while($i22 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i22], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category00 * 14) + $i22] # -1)
      set_control_par_str(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i22], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category00 * 14) + $i22]]])
      if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category00 * 14) + $i22] = %_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i22], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
      else
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i22], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
      end if
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i22], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
    inc($i22)
  end while
  $i22 := 0
  while($i22 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category) - 1)) 
    if($i22 = $category00)
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$i22], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$i22], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
    end if
    inc($i22)
  end while
  $subarticulation_browser_active_category := $category00
end function
function c_move_legato_buffer_to_instrument0
  $note_idx01 := 0
  $transition_idx01 := 0
  $dyn_layer_idx00 := 0
  while($dyn_layer_idx00 <= 1) 
    $note_idx01 := 0
    while($note_idx01 <= 127) 
      $transition_idx01 := 0
      while($transition_idx01 <= 24) 
        %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_release_time[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_wait_time[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_start[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_release_time_offset[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_wait_time_offset[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start_offset[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume_offset[($instrument70 * 204800) + (($keyswitch110 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx50 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume_offset[($dyn_layer_idx00 * 3200) + (($note_idx01 * 25) + $transition_idx01)]
        inc($transition_idx01)
      end while
      inc($note_idx01)
    end while
    inc($dyn_layer_idx00)
  end while
end function

function find_loaded_legato
  $authoring_page_active := 0
  if(%_loaded_subarticulations[0] # -1)
    if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[0]]] = 2)
      $authoring_page_active := 1
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_authoring_legato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[0]]] & " (" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & ")")
    end if
  end if
end function
